***перестроить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перестроить.html>перестро́ить</a> (18733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестроить.html>перестро́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perestróitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестраивать.html>перестра́ивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rebuild, to reconstruct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tune, to attune</li>
<li><i>(a radion)</i> to switch over</li>
<li>to reorganize, to rearrange, to reform</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to re-form</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестройка.html>перестро́йка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perestrójka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перестроение</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perestrojenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестроить.html>перестро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perestróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестроиться.html>перестро́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perestróitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестраиваться.html>перестра́иваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change one's approach/ways/policy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">radio</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to switch over <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перестроиться.html>перестро́иться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:короткий.html>коро́ткие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perestróitʹsja</b> na korótkije volny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to switch over [re-tune] to short waves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to re-form</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестроить.html>перестро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perestróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перестройка.html>перестро́йка</a> (4692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">over, over again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strójka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">construction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестройка.html>перестро́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perestrójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестройка.html>перестро́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестройка.html>перестро́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестройка.html>перестро́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rebuilding, reconstruction</li>
<li>reorganization, restructuring, reformation</li>
<li>reorientation</li>
<li>perestroika <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a program of political and economic reform carried out in the Soviet Union in the 1980s</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***перестук.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перестук.html>пересту́к</a> (19799)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пересту́кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perestúkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестук.html>пересту́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perestúk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестук.html>пересту́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестук.html>пересту́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перестук.html>пересту́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tapping</li>
<li>taping sound</li>
<li>knocking out (a message), communicating through knocking</li>
<li>knocking repeatedly, or alternately on many objects</li></ol>

***переступать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ть</a> (9692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perestupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переступить.html>переступи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to step over, to overstep, to step
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perestupátʹ</b> poróg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross [step over] the threshold</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to transgress, to break
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́цы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приличие.html>прили́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perestupátʹ</b> granícy prilíčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to transgress/overstep the bounds of decency</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to move, to walk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jedvá <b>perestupátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move step by step; move slowly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perestupátʹ</b> s nogí na nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shift from one foot to the other; shift from foot to foot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переступле́ние</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perestuplénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">преступа́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prestupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">преступи́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prestupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***переступающий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переступать.html>переступа́ющий</a> (9692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пересчитать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a> (9237)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sčitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peresčitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитывать.html>пересчи́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to recount, to count again</li>
<li>to convert <i>(to)</i> <i>(other units)</i></li>
<li>to count <i>(all)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>рёбра</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>кости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peresčitátʹ vse rjóbra; peresčitátʹ vse kosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to beat the tar, beat the stuffing <i>(out of)</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ступень.html>ступе́ни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peresčitátʹ stupéni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall down the steps</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перечесть.html>перече́сть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perečéstʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитывать.html>пересчи́тывать</a> (12218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peresčitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитывать.html>пересчи́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peresčítyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересчитать.html>пересчита́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перечесть.html>перече́сть</a></b>)

***пересылать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пересылать.html>пересыла́ть</a> (27394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сыла́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sylátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересылать.html>пересыла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peresylátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переслать.html>пересла́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send, to remit, to forward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пересылать.html>пересыла́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peresylátʹ</b> po póčte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send by post; mail</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыльный.html>пересы́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peresýlʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poslátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***пересыпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересыпа́ть</a> (20517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересы́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peresýpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересыпа́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pour <i>(from; into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересыпа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соль.html>соль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мешок.html>мешо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peresypatʹ</b> solʹ v mešók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pour off salt into a bag</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sprinkle <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><i>(speech)</i> to intersperse <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to pour too much, to put too much</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересы́пать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peresýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересыпа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peresypátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересы́пать</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pour <i>(from; into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пересыпать.html>пересыпа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соль.html>соль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мешок.html>мешо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peresypatʹ</b> solʹ v mešók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pour off salt into a bag</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sprinkle <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><i>(speech)</i> to intersperse <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to pour too much, to put too much</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***перетаскивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перетаскивать.html>перета́скивать</a> (20118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перетаск-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peretask-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетаскивать.html>перета́скивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peretáskivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетащить.html>перетащи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drag over, to carry over, to drag <i>(over)</i>, to lug <i>(across)</i>, to carry <i>(over)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перетащить.html>перетащи́ть</a> (12885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетащить.html>перетащи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peretaščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетаскивать.html>перета́скивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drag over, to carry over, to drag <i>(over)</i>, to lug <i>(across)</i>, to carry <i>(over)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a> (5881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*perti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*prey</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fare</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ferry</i> as well as German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fahren</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to trudge, to drag the feet
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигаться.html>передвига́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvigátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to travel (on a burdensome journey)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигаться.html>передвига́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvigátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry (a burden)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal, to pinch
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спереть.html>спере́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упереть.html>упере́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give off an unpleasant odour, to stink
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>От́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>прёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чеснок.html>чесноко́м</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ot tebjá <b>prjót</b> česnokóm.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You reek of garlic.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enjoy, to revel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>прёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> музла́</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Menjá <b>prjót</b> ot étovo muzlá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This music makes me revel.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> even more</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ball, to floss
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Троеразных</span> (lyrics), Reenboy (music),  “Street Credibility”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряженный.html>заря́жен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старт.html>ста́рта</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:куплет.html>купле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> ма́нтра<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a>, ба́ртер<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукаве́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:козырной.html>козырна́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рта</a><br /><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>Пру́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> ге́тте<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zarjážen so stárta<br />kuplét kak mántra<br />vrémja, délo, bártɛr<br />V rukavé kozyrnája kárta<br /><b>Pru</b> kak v gétte<br />V spínu nam véter</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Charged from the start<br />Strophe like mantra<br />Time, business, barter<br />In the sleeve a trump card<br /><b>Balling</b> as in the ghetto<br />In the back to us the wind</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переться.html>пере́ться</a> (22406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переться.html>пере́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to travel <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually far away</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shuffle, to trudge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перетягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перетягивать.html>перетя́гивать</a> (32172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перетяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peretjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетягивать.html>перетя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peretjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетянуть.html>перетяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перетягивать.html>перетя́гивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peretjágivatʹ na svojú stóronu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <i>(try to)</i> win over to one's side</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stretch again</li>
<li>to pull in tight, to bind, to gird</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull, to draw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перетягивать.html>перетя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peretjágivatʹ</b> s odnovó mesta na drugóje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull/draw from one place to another</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перетягивать.html>перетя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>берегу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peretjágivatʹ</b> lódku k beregu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull/draw the boat to the shore</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to outbalance, to overbalance, to outweigh
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перетягивать.html>перетя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чаша.html>ча́шу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>весо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peretjágivatʹ</b> čášu vesóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn/tip the scale</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
